<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:road.html>road</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:originally.html>originally</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:railway.html>railway</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jargon.html>jargon</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:overzetten.html>overzetten</a> (39064)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">oversetten</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zetten.html>zetten</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">oversætte</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">übersetzen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bokm%C3%A5l" class="extiw" title="w:Bokmål">Norwegian Bokmål</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nb">oversette</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">översätta</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">overset</i>.
